1. Application Overview
1.1 System Description
The Cricket Association Management System is a purpose-built digital platform for NDCA, consolidating player registration, club management, selection processes, match scheduling, tournament management, news, gallery, and public engagement into one unified system hosted and maintained by Indigen Services.

2.3 Layout System
All admin dashboards use a two-panel layout: a fixed left sidebar (240px) for navigation and a full-height main content area with a sticky topbar. The mobile app uses a bottom tab navigation pattern.

3. Public Website Wireframe
3.1 Full Layout
The NDCA public website is a content-rich, fully responsive site targeting fans, players, clubs, and media. All content is managed from the Admin Panel â€” no separate CMS login.

5. Club Admin â€” Mobile App
Club Admins log in via the mobile app using credentials issued by the Super Admin. They see and manage only their own club's data.

8. Login &amp; Role-Based Redirection
A single login screen handles both Super Admin (web) and Club Admin / Player (mobile app). The system auto-detects the role from credentials and redirects accordingly.

8.3 Key User Flows
Player Onboarding
Club Admin adds new player â†’ fills form + uploads documents â†’ submits to NDCA
Super Admin reviews â†’ Approve / Reject with remarks â†’ player notified via app
On approval: Player credentials auto-issued â†’ player logs in â†’ views profile + selection status
Match &amp; Live Score Flow
Super Admin creates match â†’ set teams, date, venue, format â†’ published to public website &amp; app
Match day: Super Admin updates live scores (runs, wickets, overs) â†’ auto-pushed to public feed
Match completed â†’ final result saved â†’ league standings updated automatically
Club Registration Flow
Club contacts NDCA â†’ Super Admin creates permanent club profile â†’ documents uploaded &amp; verified
Club Admin credentials issued â†’ Yearly renewal: each season re-submit renewal form â†’ approval
9. UX Best Practices
9.1 Responsive Design
Breakpoints: Mobile (&lt; 768px) | Tablet (768â€“1024px) | Desktop (&gt; 1024px)
Admin web panel: Desktop-first; sidebar collapses to hamburger on tablet
Mobile app: React Native â€” native performance on Android and iOS
Tables on mobile: Convert to card-list layout with column visibility priority
Charts: Recharts with ResponsiveContainer wrapper
9.2 Accessibility (WCAG 2.1 AA)
Colour contrast: All text meets 4.5:1 ratio minimum
Keyboard navigation: All elements reachable via Tab; visible focus ring
Touch targets: Minimum 44x44px on all mobile UI elements
Form validation: Inline error messages next to fields, not colour-only cues
Alt text: All player photos, club logos, and gallery images include descriptive alt attributes

9.4 Cricket-Specific UX Patterns
Approval flow visibility: Players and Club Admins always see exact status (Pending / Under Review / Approved / Rejected with reason)
Age group validation: DOB-based auto-assignment of U-14, U-16, U-19, Senior â€” with override alert
Live score readability: Score in large, high-contrast format â€” optimised for quick reading on mobile
Document readability: Player documents in high-contrast, print-optimised format
Trial fee tracking: Payment status shown with receipt upload option
9.5 Security UX
Session timeout: 30 minutes for Super Admin; 24 hours for Club Admin and Player apps (with biometric re-auth)
Audit trail: Super Admin sees 'last modified by' on every player record and approval action
Role confirmation: Irreversible actions (delete, archive) require confirmation dialog
Aadhaar masking: Displayed as XXXX-XXXX-3456 by default; click to reveal with audit log
10. Core Module Wireframes
10.1 League / Tournament Management
Accessible from the League Management sidebar item. Full control over all tournaments.

10.2 News &amp; Gallery Management
News: Rich-text WYSIWYG editor, category tagging, publish/schedule/unpublish, image upload, preview before publishing
Gallery: Drag-and-drop album creation, bulk photo upload, album cover selection, reorder images, delete
YouTube: Paste video URL, set thumbnail, categorise (Highlights / Announcements / Events)

A. Compliance &amp; Data Requirements
DPDP Act 2023 (India): Player Aadhaar and personal data handled with consent. Data stored in India (AWS Mumbai region). Parental consent required for players under 18.
Aadhaar Handling: Displayed masked by default. Full number stored encrypted. Access logged per UIDAI guidelines.
Audit Logs: Every admin action on player data is logged automatically â€” user, timestamp, action, affected record ID. Immutable, stored separately.
Data Backup: Daily automated backup to AWS S3. One-click manual backup. Retention: 90 days rolling.
HTTPS/SSL: All API endpoints over HTTPS. Mandatory for Play Store and App Store publishing.
